warre stede peace domynacyon rule lordshyppe stede humblenes lowlynes vsurpe empyre hole worlde yet neuertheles notwithstandynge stonde owne conceytes thynke selues haue ryght faythe chrysten lyuers dyd chryste place teache earthely empyres lordshyppes worlde coueted desyred dyd teache rather maner wayes thyng auoyded eschewed doctryne euydent surely knowen haue ben perfectlye obserued kepte true dyscyples sayde serue god also mammon ryches soeuer olde tyme dyd beleue hym duely oughte doo doubtynge nothynge thynge true theyr owne free wylles dyd forsake caste theym theyr goodes possessyons beynge heuye wayghty burthayns beynge lybertye lyghte folowed lorde lyfe whiche professed theym selues guydes blynde persones laughynge theym scorne theyr thus doynge whiche thynge moste peryllous tyme dreade nothyng selues folowe phariseys apostle sayinge moste expedyent chyefly profytable churche haue fatte ryche thynges rente profettes selfe craftely subtelly men churche dayes rather folowers phariseys ye apostle pykynge gatherynge togyther holy scrypture fewe name ryche men whiche maye maner waye holde vp strengthe maynteyne owne sentence sayinges passynge purposely none iyes faste shytte closed wonte sayde syxe hondreth place maketh contrary parte yet shall lytle dyuersyte yf man wyll dylygentlye marke take hede betwene theyr maner rychenes oures fyrste feare leaste haue gotten ryches goodes lyke moche holylye ryghtfully abraham isaach iacob iob suche dyd gette theyr substauce whiche gatte whiche wayes laboures husbondrye without hurtynge damagynge man v feare leste haue made selfes ryche withoute paynes trauayle taken owne parte menes laboure ye oftentymes greefe smarte sorowe also men besyde afore rehersed persones dyd neuer esteme thyse thynges ryches neyther whan plentyfull theym dyd sette theyr herte vpon theym doo whiche stryue kepe warre amonge selues one thyse thynges fercely veray lyfe feare therfore saye leste veray great dyuersytie betwene theym v yf man wolde ponder dylygently consydre maner gettynge vse affeccyon bothe partes sentence opynyon iudgement nothynge therfore holpen defended example deades theym whiche farre awaye elles couetousnes onely whan dydde vse thyse ryches goodes instrumentes benefycence lyberalytie euen towarde straungers nacyons whome dydde knowe moste comonly vse theym helper aydes iniuryes wronges el exercyse voluptuousnes wantonnes whan dyd haue theyr ryches accordynge sayeng paule thoughe hadde theym contrary wyse whan lyue addicted vtterly gyuen bonde vnto ar founde perceyued possessed theym rather vnto hym also gowne loue enemyes good whiche dothe hate v dare bolde denye chryste taughte dyscyples thyse thynges maye without moste euydent cryme preuarycacyon manyfest praye knowen thynges may auoyde escape crafte subtylyte say thyse thynges vnderstande thus lyterall gramaticall cense ye moreouer fercely pronouce hym herttyke forthwith soeuer shall iudge thynke true cense meanynge scrypture rather defended maynteyned coacte cense imagyned v affyrmynge oughte cleue leane exposycion declaracyon holy father wytte dunce thomas sylnester catharinus suche sorte seynge lawfull gyue credence scrypture hit selfe thyng must euery embrace cense whiche exposytor maketh moste true cense thynge pray compelled agaynst wyl gyue credence men certayne veray tryflers gyue credence god nay rather thynge anulle make voyde lawe god bynde chrysten people lust appetyte pleasure man openly fare behalfe thoughe churche coulde lenger knowe certayne gospelles haue certayne apostels prophettes nowe swerdes woll gyue ye key kyngdom heuens whatsoeuer thou shalt bynde vpon erth shall bounden also heuens c whiche thyse sayeng nowe applyed yt serueth rather sensual appetytes lust intencion purpose churche muste nedely obey peter yf thy mayster meaned wordes dydest thou whan thou made chyefe capytayne hed thy bretherne saye thyse wordes thyne owne selfe subgettes euery man loue god whether kynge excellent persone duke persones sent hym certayne one moste holy father greuously rebuketh sayth lowde voyce thou peter dydest speke thyse wordes thy self onely thy subgettes howe conuenyently metely hath founde startynge hole helpe hym selfe shulde saye soeuer peter taughte dyd reache onely wordes dayes rather moche dyd teache workes deades contynuell example folowyng poynte also custome maner lawes gouerne byddeth wylleth man gouerne vnderstande without lawe owne pleasure ioyneth putteth also beeste sheweth cause sayth lytle sayenge propter quod sine appetitu intellectus lex est shulde saye goodly sentence lawe vnderstandynge knowledge reason without appetite luste saye without affeccyon sentence repeteth also fyrst boke retorykes fyrst chapytre saythe thus conuenyent therfore well made lawes determyne thynges soeuer doth happen chaunce comytte fewe thynges arbrytrement ye iudges assygneth afore alledged cause wyt exclusyon auoydynge malyce ignoraunce iudges cyuyle iudgementes prynces ruler gouerne accordynge lawes comune weale vnderstande thou temperate well ordred lawe ought gouernoure ruler ouer nowe resteth remayneth shewe prynces gouernoures ought gouerne accordynge lawe without besyde namelye moste prynces kynges whiche made gouernours al theyr yssue ofsprynge theyr kyngdome powre maye sure maner ieopardye peryll also may endure cotynue longer whiche secondarie fynall cause necessyre lawes assygned hus begynnynge chapitre fyrste may proued gouerne rule accordynge lawes preserueth iudgmentes sayde gouernoures defaulte whiche myght happen reason ignoraunce peruerse affeccyon whiche lawes beynge guyded well ordred theyr owne selues towarde theyr comunes subiectes lesse suffre sedycyons consequentlye lesse suffre solucyons destruccyons theyr kyngdomes whiche myght happen chaunce doynge lewdlie accordynge theyr wyll pleasure arystotle sayth openlye v boke polytykes x chapytre regnum sayth saye kyngdome seldome lytle destroyed thynges whiche men preestes iudges people yt yere al notwithstadynge yet gaue false testymony wytnesse agaynst wold cosent applye selfe theyr wycked fylthie cocupyscece lust nowe therfore yf preestes aged men man wolde lytle thynke corrupted throughe catnall concupyscence howe moche couetousnes vyces thought men doubtles man neuer vertuous without peruerse corrupte affeccyon ignoraunce lawe therfore sure way neyther passyon neyther ignoraunce hym yet may sone shall subiecte synystre euyll affeccyon wherof rulynge accordynge theyr wylfull affeccyon without certayne lawe ordre may ensue moche inconuenyence whiche yf ye wyll replye saynge yt theyr father beynge good man supposed peraduenture wyl delyuer powre auctoryte answere suche sayenge beleaued regarded partlye lyeth hym depryue successyon comenlye hathe knowledge wherfore arystotle thyrde boke politikes xi chapytre answerynge obieccyon sayth wyse easye beleue wyt father wyll dysheryte owne sone kyngdome powre harde thynge greatter worthy reproue reason wherof theyr kyngdome powre shall made sure daunger also contynuall durable cause counsayle excellent phylosopher arystotle vnto prynces gouernours wherof take lytell heade vnto hym wherfore haue iudged conuenyent brynge texte wordes arystotle syngularyte excellent vertue prynce suche neuer maner hath ben herde space many hendreth yeres haue ben prynce wordes arystotle profytable thynges whiche instytuted ordayned yet maye dyscerne iudge sayd thynges beynge inuented men purposed moued vnto whether yf thynge seme added mynysshed vtterlye chaunged dyspysed refused wyt alone inuencyon fyrste fyndynge thynges harde wherfore arystotle saythe seconde boke eleuches last chapytre harde thynge fynde fyrst begynnynge trouth begynniges thynges harde founde maner dyscyplyne scyece ye begynnige beyng one foude easy thynge adde put resydue wherfore fynde begynnynges pryncyples scyences artes tradycyons appertayneth vnto men best moste sharpe wyttes thynges whiche inuented redy men course grosse wyt may adde called herfore vndyscrete fooles inuete fynde suche thynges selues theyr owne wyttes rather ought accompted nombre good men sayde arystotle fyrst hym ii qualytes departed dysseuered one wyt prudence morall vertue namely iustyce ryghtuousnes one wyt prudence necessarie ende mynde vnderstandynge hym may dyrected gouernynge exercysynge offyce whiche vertue iustyce conuenyent hym shal gouernoure certayne vertue assocyated called epicikeia vertue iudge dyrected equyte mekenes gentylnes extremytie cruelnes specyallye cheyfly thynges wherin operacyon prynce gouernoure causynge hym sustayne suffre payne ponysshemente therfore penalyte ponysshemet certayne medycyne cryme trespase wherfore arystotle seconde boke etykes thyrde chapytre ceaseth albeit accyons partes cyuyle comunyte may somtyme cease without noyaunce hurte syngulare persone colledge comunyte example operacyon men warre maye cease tyme peace lykewyse operacyons partes punysshed secular iudge yet thomas cau turbery wolde haue prynce preest bysshop hath ben shewed iiii v chapytours dyccyon therfore bysshoppes preestes beynge trasgressoures mane lawe oughte punysshed prince gouernour onely preeste spyrytuall mynyster ought punysshed secular man transgressyon lawe also ought punysshed moch greuously largely howe moche offence heynouse vnsemynge lesse defended doth synne knowyngly election whiche oughte knowe preceptes thynges done eschewed agayne offence shamefull hym whiche ought teache hym whiche oughte taughte preest whiche ought teache laye man whiche oughte lerne wherfore preeste offendeth greuouslye therfore sore punysshed laye man neyther obiection oughte obiectyon sprytualtie answered vnto receyued alowed whiche wolde say maner iniuries verball reall personall suche thynges prohybyted mane lawe yf done agaynst man preest accyons spyrytuall therfore dothe appertayne belonge prynce seculer gouernoure punysshe preest suche offence trespass suche maner thynges prohybyted lawe aduoutrye maymynge murther thefte robbery dyffamacyon detraction treason fraude gyle heresye suche crymes comytted done preeste carnall temporall dedes offence verye well knowen experyence haue declared heretofore seconde chapytre dyccyon auctorytie apostle thyrde chapytre fyrste epystle corynthians xv romayns ye also iudged moche carnall temporall offenc howe moche preest bysshop comyttynge synneth greuously shamefully ought call backe suche offence gyuynge occasyon theym redynesse offende trespasse throughe lewde vngracyous example p therfore euery preeste bysshoppe vndre ought vndre iurysdyccyon prynces secular gouernours thynges whiche comaunded obserued lawe man aswell seculare laye men neyther bysshoppe preeste exempted coactyue iudgement suche prynces neyther maye exempte man owne auctoryte whiche thynge proue addycyon thynges whiche hath ben sayd xvii chapytre fyrste dyccyon dedusynge bryngynge hym whiche doth saye contrary ameruaylous great inconuenyent yf bysshop rome pope rome exempte fro iurysdyccyon offeculare prynces preeste exempted shulde vndre coactyue rysdyccyon prynces gouernours hym selfe suche maner iudge without auctorytye humayne lawe maker myght seperate exempte ye sprytuall mynysters ye comune name call clarkes iurysdyccyon prynces gouernours make subiectes hym selfe bysshoppes rome done nowe dayes folowed necessarylye iurysdyccyon seculer gouernours maner vtterly adnulled destroyed made strength whiche thynge recounte great inconuenyent intollerable gouernours comunyties chrysten relygyon dothe depryue man ryght shewed afore auctorytie ambrose vpon sayenge paule seconde chapytre titus admonysshe subiectes prynces powres c brought alledged v chapytre dyccyon inconuenyent dothe folowe suche exempcyon thus proue founde prohybyted goddes lawe rather graunted also lawful hym preeste bysshop whiche hath wyfe namely yf haue mo wyues one redde thyrde chapytre fyrst epystle tymothe whiche decreed ordayned mannes lawe constytucyon maye auctorytie reuoked adnulled mannes lawe therfore bysshop rome maketh hym selfe lawe maker maye fulnes powre yf man wyll graunte hym haue ful powre graunte preestes deacon subdeacon haue wyues maye graunted preest haue wyues onely also whiche haue taken foresayd ordres otherwyse consecrated whome call clarkes syngle tonsure yea moreouer semyngly whiche thynge bonifacius viii semeth haue done dede myght increase seculer powre hym selfe many hadde maryed virgyne whiche wyllynge wedde one wyfe ascrybed company charkes decreed shuld ascrybed ordynacyons constytucyons call decretales neyther kepynge within boundes haue exempted cyuyle lawes man duely made certayne laye men whome call italy fratres gaudentes place called begymes haue also exempted fratres gaudetes begini bretherne called fratres hospitaliorum templariorum brethern hospytalles templar many suche lyke order lykewyse whiche called dealto passu also theyr pleasure myghte lyke maner lyke reason wherfore yf maner men exempte iurysdyccyon prynces gouernours accordynge theyr decretales also gyueth persones exempted certayne lybertyes imunytes publyke cyuyle charg burthaynes semeth lykelye greater multytude parte men shall declyne company namelye seynge take receyue indyfferentlye relygyous men receyue men lerned theyr order learned vnlerned euery man prone redye folowe drawe owne profyte auoyde eschewe owne dysprofyte yf greater multytude men shall declyne company clarkes shall iurysdyccyon coactyue powre prynces remayne strength weake feble whiche great inconuenyence thynge wherby comune wealth cyuyle gouernaunce shulde destroyed soeuer enioyeth cyuyle honour comodytyes profytes peace defence cheyfe gouernour ought exempte cyuyle charg burtheyns cyuyle iurysdyccyon without determynacyon gouernoure aduoydynge therfore great inconuenyent oughte graunte accordynge vnto trouthe hyghe cheyfe gouernoure hath iurysdyccyon vpon bysshoppes preestes clarkes leste myght chaunce good ordre comune weale broken pluralytie cheyfe gouernoures beynge one vndre determytted xvii fyrste dyccyon cheyfe gouernour ought determyne apoynte certayne nombre prouynce vnder gouernaunce lykewyse dothe persones parte comune weale lefte yf dyd growe vp ouer greate multytude myght able resyste coactyue powre gouernours otherwyse great dysturbauce comune weale elles theyr pryde ouer great multytude depryue cytie realme comunytye profyte auauntage theyr necessarye workes occupacyons outwarde actes dedes goynge tournynge profyte dysprofyte ryght wronge sondry persone doer ought ruled measured humayne lawe iudge thyrde sygnyfycacyon whiche coactyue iurysdyccyon seculer laye men also charkes oughte subiectes also iudges accordynge lawes lawyer man whiche called iudges fyrste secode sygnyfycacion ye teacher lawes yet lackynge wantynge coactiue powre auctorytie whiche sorte thynge letteth may many ordred one vnder euen one communytie p relacyon respecte mannes dedes workes vnto lawe god iudge worlde wytte chryste also howe dedes ar compared teacher lawe wytte bysshoppe preeste worlde ix chapytre accordynge therfore maner also certayne iudge hauynge coactyue iurysdyccyon auctoryte vpon transgressours lawe god whiche lawe also haue sayde coactyue rule dedes workes men well whiche called actus imanentes whiche called actus transeuntes iudge one wytte chryste none wherfore wryten iiii chapytre iames one lawe maker whiche maye dystroye delyuer coactyue one lawe maker chryste powre iudge exersysed vpon man world towchynge dystrybucyon payne rewarde transgressours obseruers lawe imedyatly gyuen hym whiche often tymes haue called lawe gospell chryste great mercy wolde graunte vnto v space wherin myghte penaunce synnes comytted agaynst lawe euen vntyll laste ende euery mannes lyfe shall shewed hereafter also auctorytes holy scrypture also scrypture gospell iudge fyrst sygnyfycacyon lykewyse mannes iudge taken preacher lawe wytte preest whiche worlde teacher goddes lawe suche thynges whiche eyther done eschewed gettynge eternall lyfe aduoydynge payne eternall yet hauynge coactyue powre worlde copell man obseruynge iudge hath coactyue powre preceptes comaundementes lawe shuld vayne none effecte compell man vnto obseruynge hym shulde obserue onely compulsyon shulde nothynge auayleable clargy many yere hath done copulsyon swerde fyre vnto eternall helthe shewed euydently auctorytie chrysostome also apostle paule v chapytre dyccyon therfore iudge conuenyentlye lykened physycyon leche whiche hathe auctorytie gyuen hym teache comaunde prenostycate iudge thynges whiche profytable done lefte vndone optaynynge gettynge bodely helthe aduoydynge death syckenesse whiche shulde chaunce hym whiche cause chryste also state state presente lyfe called hym selfe physycyon leche prynce iudge therfore sayd vnto pharyseys speakyng hym selfe brought chapytre afore gone nede leche whiche helthe whiche sycke dyseased chryste hath ordayned man shulde compelled worlde obseruacyon lawe made hym therfore hathe ordayned iudge spyrytuall hauynge coactyue powre punysshe transgressours lawe worlde wherfore marked taken hede lawe gospell may two maner wayes compared vnto men vpon whome made chryste one waye maye compared state state presente lyfe comparyson maye rather called speculatyue practyue doctryne elles bothe lawe taken propre last sygnyfycacyon albeit maye called lawe sygnyfycacyons worde seconde thyrde sygnyfycacyons whiche haue spoken x chapytre fyrste dyccyon cause whiche haue sayde name worde lawe thyrde sygnyfycacyon belongeth onelye coactyue rule wytte rule accordynge whiche transgressoure punysshed powre coactyue gyuen hym whiche ought iudge accordynge rule nowe lawe gospell lawe maker therof comaunded man shulde compelled spyrytuall man worlde obserue thynges whiche comaunded lawe done lefte vndone worlde therfore beynge compared state man worlde worlde ought called doctryne lawe onely suche maner haue sayde mynde apostle thyrde chapytre seconde epystle tymothe scrypture inspyred god aboue profytable teache argue proue rebuke instructe ryghtuousnesse neuer sayde profytable compelle punysshe worlde wherfore fyrste chapytre seconde epystle corynthyanes apostle sayth lordes gouernours ouer faythe helper comforter ioye stande faythe saynt ambrose haue shewed v chapytre dyccyon greueth reherse often tymes agayne sayth wordes lest corynthyanes myght mysco tent ambrose angrye yf apostle taken vpon hym lorde ouer sayd sparynge haue come therfore apostle sayth followyngely saye aforesayd wordes sparynge fayth suffereth domynyon compulsyon fayth voluntarye whiche thynge freewyll necessytye speake wordes therfore helper yf wyll worke v c loo sayth helper wyt doctryne saythe also yf wyll worke v whiche nowe stande faythe worketh loue domynyon compulcyon maner way scryture lawe yf men seme punysshed breakynge goddes lawe world comittige aduoutry nycacio theft heresy forth malyce theyr hert breketh forth disqeteth theyr neyghbours therby offe deth ye kyng lawe respecte offende goddes lawe whiche onely referred god punysshed euerlastigly gospell maye compared vnto men state worlde whiche worlde onely shal payned punysshed whosoeuer hath transgressed broken sayd lawe worlde maye well called lawe moste propre sygnyfycacion iudgeth accordynge whiche chryste maye called iudge moste propre sygnyfycacyon worde hathe coactyue powre thyrde sygnyfycacyon worde preeste bysshop euer asmoche dothe rule ordre men accordynge lawe onely state presente lyfe althoughe lyfe come neyther graunted hym imedyate maker lawe wyt chryste punysshe man accordynge worlde therfore preeste bysshop called iudge properly thyrde sygnyfycacyon whiche hathe coactyue powre neyther maye neyther ought punysshe man suche maner iudgement worlde eyther reale personall payne punysshement lyke maner doctour teacher operatyue physycyon comparyson iudgement bodely helth men hauynge powre coactyue man haue sayde aboute begynnynge present chapytre also sentence saynt iohn crysostome playnlye openly agreynge mynde apostle fyrste chapytre seconde epystle corynthyanes boke dyaloges whiche also entytled dygnytie preesthode seconde boke thyrde chapytre ordre wordes haue brought heretofore vi parte v chapytre dyccion haue rehersed agayne cause shortnesse wordes whiche folowe nexte aforesayde texte haue put cause moch nede sayth helpe crafte conynge men may perswaded brought mynde whan sycke theyr owne accorde frewyll offre selfe leche crafte physyke preestes onelye also preestes maye good gentle cured whether man chrysostome wolde starte backe whan bounde verely thynge hath powre free lybertye shall make dysease worse whether wyl refuse word whiche shulde haue done hym good stede surgeans salues instrumentes ioyneth addeth wounde vnto fyrst wounde reason cotempte occasyon therof becomed vnto hym selfe instrument peryllous deadely dysease man maye cure heale one agaynst wyll sayd chrysostome certayne wordes added hym consernynge correccyon amendement people marked al curat cosernynge ye copellynge costraynige sayth word yf man led ye right fayth tha remayneth preest appertayneth charge vse moch exhortacion moch wyse dylygence moch pacyence may brynge man agayne nota faythe vyolence shall enforce hym selfe vttermoste endeuoure perswade suche persone yt wyll retourne ryght fayth whiche hath fyrst fallen lo howe holy man doth seperate departe iudgement preestes iudgement prynces gouernours coactyue iudgement neyther dothe belonge neyther ought belonge preestes assygnynge cause whiche haue sayde oftentymes heretofore fyrste coactyue power gyuen temporall lawe elles law maker prynce whiche graunted preestes chrysostomes tyme prouynce secondaryly yf suche coactyue power shuld graunted vnto euen pyte grauted tyme wherein many tyraunt clergye yet shulde vayne exercyse vpon theyr subiectes spyrytuall thynge auayleth men compelled vnto neyther profyteth whyt eternall helthe sayd vpon texte ix luke yf man wylleth come lette hym denye hym selfe haue lefte ordre wordes partely aforesayd suffycyent partely cause shortenesse also plyanely openlye mynde saynt hilarie constantius emperour whiche epystle amonge thynges thus wrote emperoure god hath taughte knowlege hym selfe rather hathe exacted gettynge admyracyon hilarius estymacyon preceptes heuenly workes despysed refused maner auctorytie coactyue men confesse knowlege hym selfe loo god wylleth men taughte knowynge confessyng hym wytte fayth man compelled therto despyseth reherseth agayne longe sayeng god requyreth coacte confessyon agayne afterwarde persone preestes saythe thus receyue man excepte wyllynge hilarius man prayeng sygne marke man hym professeth therfore god wyll haue coacte confessyon owne selfe neyther wylleth man drawen therunto violence hym compulsyon wherfore hilarius agaynst auxentius bysshop mylayne reputed arriane whiche procured men co pelled force armes sayde hilarius saythe confesse thynges feare hath yet many arrians yf myghte haue fulswynge swerde theyr handes whiche belonged owne opynyon aboute rather agaynst fayth rebukynge hym albeit ben taughte thynge trouthe sayth thus fyrste maye petye laboure trauayle tyme age sorowe bewayle folysshe opynyons tymes whiche worldly thynges supposed beleued helpe defende god laboured seculare ambycyon defence mayntayne churche chryste agayne persone place sayth ala pytie erthly helpes aydes comende fayth god causeth accepted chryste proued without powre might whyles ambycion ioyned name church putteth men feare tyme punysshe hilarius rayleth agaynste clargye banysshementes prysons copelleth men gyue credence vnto beleued banysshementes prysonamentes hilarius speaketh churche vnderstadynge colledge copany preest bysshoppes mynysters churche whome call comenlye clarkes also openly mynde saynt ambrose valentiane ye emperour seconde epystle whiche intytled comune people whan sayde ambrose may wepe may sory may mourne syghe agaynst wepons armour agaynst men warre agaynst bothians teares wepons suche armoure preestes otherwyse neyther ought neyther may resyste beholde preeste ought althoughe myghte moue stereany wepon power coactyue agaynst man neyther yet comaunde exorte wepons power coactyue moued namelye agaynst chrysten men contrarye wherof worlde maye worlde comaunded compelled spyrytualtie payne punysshement embracynge obseruacyon preceptes lawe gospell neyther infydell yet vninfydel wherfore mynystres lawe bysshoppes preestes neyther maye iudge man worlde iudgement thyrde sygnyfycacion neyther compell man obserue preceptes goddes lawe namely without auctorytie humayne lawe maker suche maner iudgement accordynge lawe god ought exercysed worlde execusyon therof done onely worlde come wherfore xix mathewe ihesus sayd vnto apostle suertye saye vnto whiche haue folowed regeneracyon whan sone man shall sytte seate maiestye also shall sytte vpon twelue seates iudgynge xii trybes israell maye ye se whan apostle shall sytte chryste iudges hym thyrde sygnyfycacion verely worlde come world glose sayth regeneracion say whan deed men shall ryse incoruptyble wherfore mynde glose two regeneracyons fyrste water holy ghost seconde generall resurreccyon wherfore vpon wordes also shall sytte saythe glose mynde augustyne whan fourme seruaunte wytte chryste whiche worlde iudged coactyue power dyd iudge shall exercyse power iudge wytte resurrection shall also iudges p loo accordynge sayeng chryste gospell exposycion sayntes chryste hathe exercysed iudicare power wytte coactyue power worlde rather beyng fourme seruaunt iudged suche maner iudgement also whan shal exercyse suche iudicare power coactyue worlde apostle also shal sytte hym iudge suche maner iudgement afore tyme bysshoppes takevpon auctory tie chryste p wherfore hit worthely greatly meruayled wherfore bysshop preeste euer shulde take vpon wyll haue greatter auctorytie worlde chryste apostle wolde haue fourme seruauntes haue ben iudged seculate worldly prynces successoures preestes bysshoppes onely refuseth subiectes prynces contrarye example precepte chryste obstynat thomas cauterbury otherwyse called thomas beket apostle also saye theym selues aboue prynces hyghest power coactyue iurysdyccion prynces subiectes vnto withstondyng chryste sayd x actes apostle cause also god gaue hym lawe thynges obserued state presente lyfe contaynynge specyally preceptes thynges departynge endynge contencions stryfes amonge men beynge moche lyke vnto lawe man touchynge parte obseruynge kepynge whiche preceptes men compelled constrayned worlde moyses substytutes coactyue iudges payne punysshement preeste appereth euydently xviii chapytre exodus chryste hathe gyuen suche preceptes lawe gospell supposed alredy gyuen shulde afterwarde gyuen lawes men whiche lawes comaunded obserued also gouernours accordynge lawes obeyed euery soule lestwyse thynges whiche shuld co trary lawe euerlastynge helthe therfore sayth xxii mathewe xi marke gyue cesare thynges belonge cesare vnderstandynge cesare maner prynce gouernoure alsothe apostle xiii romaynes saythe greueth reherse agayne let euery soule subiecte hygher powres also last chapytre fyrste epystle timothe byddeth seruauntes obedyent theyr lordes ye thoughe infydeles glose also place mynde augustyne agreeth whiche haue brought afore ye viii parte v chapytre dyccyon auctoryties appereth euydently intencyon mynde chryste apostle sayntes al men ought subiecte obedyent lawes men iudges accordynge lawes p moreouer aforesayd thynges euydent chrysten men ye precept ye olde lawe ar obserued bounde obserue kepe thyng olde lawe testament counsayled comaunded people iewes kepte obseruacyon certayne thynges whiche comaunded iewes vtterly forbydden chrysten men example seremonyes vnder payne eternall perdycyon apostle teacheth iii vii chapytres romaynes seconde v galathianes seconde ephesyanes vii x chapitres hebrues whose mynde saynt ierome saynt augustyne agreynge say theyr epystles sent one xi xiii concordynge eche obseruers suche ceremonyes outher truely faynedly publysshynge lawe gospel shal cast downe ye dogyon ye deuyl lykewyse also christen men ar boude ye obseruacyon ye legales appereth ye apostle also augustine augustyne vpon yt sayeng aforesayd last chapitre timothe whan sayd let chrysten seruaunt requyre yt requyre whiche sayde hebrues c asmoche lawe grace preceptes specyally gyuen cotencyons debatefull act men worlde determyned ended lefte thynges ought determyned lawes men iudges accordynge lawes hauynge auctorytie humayue lawe maker prynce also certayne thynges lawe moyses comauded obserued state ye worlde come preceptes sacryfyces certayne hostes oblacyos made redempcyon synnes namely preuye synnes whiche co mytted inwarde actes iudgement accomplysshynge preceptes man compelled constrayned payne punysshement present worlde lyke vnto al counseyles precept newe lawe chryste neyther wolde neyther comaunded man copelled obseruacyon worlde albeit dothe comaunde generall comaundement ordynaunces mennes lawes shulde obserued yet vnder payne punysshement done vnto transgressours worlde hym wherfore transgressours breaket mannes lawe yea punysshed world prynce maner parte trespasseth agaynst lawe god contrary wyse many actes doth leueth vndone trespasseth agaynste lawe god whiche comaundeth suche thynges wherof gyue comaundement lawes men vayne dedes whiche haue called inwarde actes neuer brastynge forth whiche proued man hym yet hyd vnknowen god therfore lawe god conuenyently gyuen suche thynges duely done lefte vndone goodnes men presente worlde also world come p peraduenture man wyll reken imperfeccyon doctryne gospell yf haue sayde contencyons debatefull actes men suffycyently ruled state state present lyfe let v saye doctryne lawe gospell suffycyent lyfe euerlastynge gospell suffycyentlye dyrected thynges done thynges auoyded eschewed present lyfe state world come eyther gettynge euerlastynge lyfe ye auoydynge escapynge euerlastynge punysshement whiche endes purpose scrypture made worldly reducynge contentious dedes men vnto equalytie dewe comensuracyon concernynge state suffycyencie present lyfe chryste came worlde rule strayghten suche maner dedes present lyfe onely lyfe come therfore rule temporall worldly actes men ben sondry maners dyuerse facyons dyrectynge vnto endes one saye lawe god teacheth wyse ought stryue go law aske owne agayne afore iudge albeit doth forbyd therfore gyueth specyall preceptes suche thynges haue sayd afore rule actes dedes wyt lawe man teacheth thynges comaundeth transgressours punysshed wherfore xii luke whan certayne man desyred chryste worldly temporall iudgement betwene hym brother chryst made answere thou man hath ordayned iudge deuyder betwene c yf sayde come exercyse temporall iudgement wherfore glose sayth dothe vouche saue iudge sutes stryffes lawe iudge vmpere worldly good substaunces whiche hath iudgement bothe quycke deed arbytrement therfore actes dedes men coulde sufficyently measured ruled lawe god euangelycall lawe ende presente worlde dede comensuratyue rule suche dedes proporcyon men lawfully desyre ye state present lyfe ben taught lawe supposed eyther gyuen elles gyuen taughte lawes men without also defaulte lacke iustice myght chaunce throughe occasyon contencyon men fyghtynge seperacyon departynge insuffycyencie mannes lyfe world thynge maner men hate auoyde naturally sayd therfore accordynge trouthe lawe doctryne gospell vnperfyte ordayned apte haue ye perfeccyon worldly mater made gyuen imedyatlye shulde dyrected cocernynge thynges thynges whiche belonge obtaynynge gettynge ye se lacke necessary vnwryten vanytyes verity wolde saye ye scrypture perfite suffycient auctoure affyrmeth euerlastynge saluacyon auoydynge euerlastynge mysery whiche thynges suffycyent perfyte made determynynge cyuyle contencyous busynes mater appertaynynge ende whiche men desyre lawfully worldly lyfe truely yf shulde called vnperfyte therfore myght called conuenyentlye vnperfyte taughte hele bodelye dyseases semely hym yf prynce gouernoure ouer people shulde counsayle exhorte men state pouertie humble lowe state agayne yf man strycken one cheke shulde holde cheke stryker also hym whiche taketh away cote ought gyue also gowne rather go lawe stryue iudge hym hathe wronged v men wolde lyghtly gyue credence hym suche thyng state whiche settynge semely hym whiche dothe also beare shulde clene contrary wroge yf shuld preache yt iniuryes forgyuen ye doer shulde gyue euyl men certayne occasyon largely trespassynge doynge euyll also ye sone offended haue suffred iniury wroge shulde gyue occasyon doubte mystruste obtaynige true iustice cause chryste hath ordayned al thig alwayes best wyse maner wold ye offyc prync gouernours preest ioyned togyther one sone rather deted one ye executed dyuerse son referred subiecte one thynge wylled done gyuynge comaudement sayde passyuely nowne precepte taken actyuely comenlye sayde ordynaunce statute prynce gouernour aswell affyrmatyue negatyue statute byndynge transgressour payne punysshement properly vsage worde nowe dayes taken onely statute affyrmatyue affyrmatyue statute hath propre name belongyng selfe vse hathe kepte selfe comen name precepte prohybycion worde prohybicion sayde two maner wayes actyuely passyuely euen lykewyse worde precepte two ordynacyons byndynge transgressoure vnto payne moste parte expressed lawes eyther accordynge whiche byndeth eternall payne maner deuynes vsen wordes saye preceptes necessyte helthe saluacyon saye nedely obserued yf man ought saued wherfore red xviii luke yf thou wylte entre lyfe kepe comaundementes saye preceptes certayne ordynauces expressed vnderstanden onely lawes affyrmatyue also negatyue eyther aboute one acte aboute dyuers sondrye actes done bynde doer el hym leueth vndone thyng ben laufull lawe man whiche laufull lawe god backewarde agayne many thyng laufull accordynge lawe god laufull accordynge lawe man howbeit yt lauful vnlauful taken hede iudged aft er law god whiche call ius takynge worde former sygnyfycacion laste rehersed nowe vsus rei vsus fructus rei laufull handlyng thynge ryght let supposed knowen cyuyle lawe present tyme sygnyfycacion wonte saye dominion englysshe moch say lordshyp worde domynyon taken straytly specyally one sygnyficacion betokeneth pryncypall powre auctoryte chalenge clayme yt optayned law ryght takynge worde ryght fyrst sygnyficacion meane ye powre hym knoweth dysagreueth wylleth also shal laufull man hadle occupye thynge without expresse co sente hym wyt lorde owner longe lorde owner powre nothynge el actuall habituall wyll haue thynge gotten ryght lawe haue sayd truely called ryght man conformable lawe ryghte takynge worde ryght fyrst sygnyfycacion whiche maner sayd pyller called ryght left pyller whan shall truely copared touchynge nerenesse vnto ryght lefte part man sensyble creature p agayne nowne domynion sayd generally powre afore rehersed whether yt powre shall vpon thynge onely el onely vpon vse takynge frute profyte comynge vsage occupyenge thynge el vpon thyng togyther p agayne nowne domynion also sayd aforesayd powre belongynge man yet knowynge cosentynge neyther expressely dysagreynge renouncynge maner thynge somwhat belongynge thynge may gotten infaute one absente persone beynge ignoraute yet beyng apte receyue domynion also powre chalenge sayd thynge hym taketh away demaunde make clayme afore iudge outher hymselfe stede sayd dysse tynge renouncynge expressely hym doth expressely disagre renounce forsake thynge vsage profyte thynge thyng gotten recouered neyther domynion powre chalenge maner man may yf lyste lawfully renounce ryght lawe broughte hym lawes man neyther man lawe copelled receyue benefyte lawe agaynst wyl domynios wherof haue nowe spoken legale domynions gotten maye gotten ordynaunce lawe possession p nowe consequently sygnyfycacions worde possessio shewed declared whiche worde possessyon taken largely betokeneth one way word domynion betokeneth fyrst seconde thyrde sygnyfycacion el betokeneth teporall thynge coparyson hym yt hath el wyllynge haue wyse maner hath ben sayde two fyrst sygnyfycacions worde domynion wherfore red xiii chapytre genesis sygnyfycacion phylosophers vse name yet moste comunelye qualyte whiche deperted subiecte subiecte p nowne comune touchynge purpose tyme taken comune cotraryly two last rehersed sygnyfycacions worde propre nowe resteth remayneth shewe many maner wayes nownes ryche pore ar take vsed p nowne ryche comunely sayd hym called ryche hath hym selfe superhabundauce superfluyte teporal thyng call ryches maner tyme present come laufully p another maner waye called ryche man whiche hath lawfully vnto hym selfe foresayd thynges onely suffycyent quantyte tyme present tyme come yet agayn nowne ryche sayd two maner wayes properly p fyrst hym hath thynges aforesayde superhabundantlye suffycientlye wyllynge also haue sayd thyng suche maner facyon p waye sayd hym hath thyng nowe sayd rehersed onely suffyciently sayde seconde sygnyfycacion worde hym wyllynge haue suffycient maner p nowne poore two fyrste sygnyfycacions dyffereth poore signyficacios worde ryche pryuacion differeth habite p one waye called poore whiche wanteth onelye superhabundaunce superfluite goodes althoughe haue suffycyentlye p waye called poore whiche hathe togyther one tyme suffycient thyng euery maner tyme yt wyt bothe presente also come p thyrde waye called poore whiche fre wyl without copulcion wyllynge berefte superabundauce superfluite goodes euery maner tyme maner sygnyfycacion worde pore dyffereth worde ryche one cotrarye contrarye p iiii way called poore wyllynge haue togyther one tyme moche suffycyent euerye maner tyme bothe present also come otherwhyles wyll owne fre wyll lacke wante wherfore euery sygnyfycacion worde pore pouertye dyfferynge contrarye euery sygnyfycacyon worde ryche indyfferentlye ought ouerhyppe whiche wyllynge poore whiche forsake temporall thynges honest ende xvi chapytre begynnynge thynges afore determyned shall chapytre fyrst shewe none apostle prehemynence aboue essencyal dygnyte preesthode tha ti wytte gyuen chryste shall shewe none instytucyon whiche haue called secondarie moche lesse iurysdyccion coactyue howbeit laste thynge hath ben suffycientlye proued iiii v chapytours dyccyon thyng shall also necessyte coclude yt none bysshops successours apostle syngularlye haue auctorytes powres aforesayd vpon ouer felowe bysshoppes felowe preestes contrarye hereof proued vertue wordes holy scrypture rather present purpose laste hereof whiche thynge sygnyfycacions appereth bysshop rome toke fyrst tytle fulnes powre vnto hym selfe viii sygnyfycacion begynnynge apparente appertaynynge therof vnto hym sayenge chryste whiche xxi iohn speakynge vnto saynt peter saythe fede shepe agayne sayd syngulerly peter xvi mathewe shall gyue keyes kyngdom heuens c agayne sayd peter xviii iohn turne thy sworde thy scaberde moreouer ye answere whiche dyscyples rome specyall vycar saynt peter apostle bysshops successours vnyuersyte whole flocke shepe whole worlde eche one one determynate pertyculare flocke prouynce hath ben comytted gouerned p bysshop rome taken vnto hym selfe tytle fulnes powre albeit accordynge trewe sence scrypture shall suffycyentlye shewed xxviii chapytre dyccyon presumpcion went sygnyfycacyon peraduenture lucre auauntage elles vsurpe comodyte profyte excellencie aboute men wyt takynge vpon hym selfe preachynge openly alone seuerallye maye maner soeuer shall please hym worde vtterlye exempte delyuer assoyle synners paynes purgatorye calleth p sygnyfycacions taken vnder certayne coloure appetaunce pytie mercye ende fyrste myght seme charyte take thought care men secondaryly myght supposed haue powre wyllynge haue mercy pytie vpon al men bysshops rome beynge stregthed pryuyleges grauntes emperours lowedely lye cheyfly emperyal seate beynge vacante dyd extende stretche forth tytle fyrst ordeynynge makynge certayne lawes vpon clarkes preestes concernynge ecclesiasticall customes ceremonyes whiche begynnynge called decree afterwardes howe wherfore fastynges certayne kyndes meates certayne dayes cam fyrste vp ordynaunces whiche sayd haue ben requestes exhortacyons tyrantes rome began comaunde openly thyng maner precepte law bolde without ye lycece colour religyon hath spro ge moch myschefe worldly prynces stryke trangressoures therof terroure drede theyr curse excomunycacyon yet vnder coloure apperaunce relygyon honorynge god afterwardes theyr appetytes hauynge mynyon increasynge whan perceyued also deuout chrysten men greatly put feare suche maner wordes throughe ignoraunce foloweth folysshe feare fonde obieccyons wyse men day ben nowe fearefulnes ignoraunce lawe god whiche beleued selues bounde vnto thynges whiche comaunded preestes feare eternall dethe bysshoppes rome theyr companye clarkes presumed statute make certayne oblygarchicall decree ordinacyons concernynge cyuyle actes whiche therunto myght enioye imunite fredom comune publyke charge reason wherof made lytle parte cyuyle multytude subiect vnto selues withdrawynge powre gouernauce seculare prynces gouernours agayne vnto haue ben taken vnto companye clarkes defamynge also openlye church dothe iniurye clarkes excomunycacyon lesse persuynge men therfore requyre haue punysshed penaltes cursynges money temporall corinthyans yet beynge contente herewith desyrynge domynyon hyghest gouernaunce seculare men contrarye precepte chryste apostle hath braste forthe makynge lawes seuerally lawes whole comunaltyes alledgynge sure vndoubted experyence therof sayd pluralyte hedes hyghest gouernours rote begynnynge pestylence dystruccyon empyre italy whiche rote hurtes occasyons euyls hathe cause vndoyng italye fearynge least powre shulde reuoked hym emperour without cause excess comytted hym wycked dylygence forbyddeth letteth treason creacyon promotynge emperour rome laste one hathe braste forthe great boldnes hath decree expressed emperour rome bounde hym othe fydelyte beynge subiecte hym coactyue iurysdyccyon appereth euydently lyfte shameles chyldren loke vpon folysshe vtterly despyse worthy vii worlde entende theyr lawes cause durst expresse begynnynge ye name lawes fered resystence correccyon aforsayd prync treason doynge comytted agaynst prynces gouernours p agayn spyrytual lawes named doth vse hetherto lykelyhode wyl vse hereafter yf stopped letted fyrst howe haue vsed instytucyon ecclesyastycall offycers dystrybutynge ecclesiastycall temporalles benefyces well vnto ecclesyastical mynystres vnto myserable persones whose cause also ecclesyastycal temporalles hath ben gyuen ordayned dystributed dysposed mynystres churche afterward shewed haue vsed hetherto doth vse hereafter wyll chryste haue dymynysshed corrupted fynally maner haue vtterly destroyed taken awaye eleccyon whiche beste waye ye moreouer whiche way onely securyte well instytutynge maner offycer notwithstandynge cause example prelate euery syde infected nere corrupcyon p nowe speake forme fascyon body whiche forme ought co syste ordre dewe sytuacyon mebres dody hym yt luste dylygently beholde aduyse marke well shall seme euyll fauored mysshapen monstre man wolde iudge bodye yt beast similitude mysshapen vnprofytable couenyent operacions whiche body euery one mebres therof imedyatly ioyned knytte vn heed ye fynger hande yf ioyned knytte imedyatly vnto heed wanteth due place shall want also vertue conuenyent mouynge operacyon shall yf fynger ioyned hande hande arme arme sholder sholder necke necke knytte heed conuenyet ioyntes body made comly shap heed maye sende couenyent vertue mebres one accordynge nature ordre sayd membres ye reason hereof may operacions couenyent belongynge vnto selues whiche forme maner ought regarde euerye bothe ecclesiasticall also cyuyle regyment gouernaunce bysshop rome imedyatly beholde loke vpon syngulare pertyculare actes euery pertyculare persone prouynces imedyatlye dyrecte yf thynges shulde done suffycyently accordyngly ought holpen specyall mynystres accordynge due ordre body churche beynge ordred may contynue also encrease whiche thynge paule doctor gentyles perceyuynge sayde wyse iiii chapytre ephesyans let v growe hym whiche poyntes heed chryste whome whole body beynge co pacted knytte togyther euery ioynte submynystracyon accordynge operacyon euery parte measure maketh increase bodye fulnes powre permytted vnto bysshop rome ordre dewe forme taken awaye alsolueth prelate archebysshops bysshoppes chaptours collegyes abbottes freers monkes pryours relygyous house theyr allegias due vnto theyr prynce hath subdued al owne cure imedyate correccyon euydent profyte vtylyte rather openly knowen greadynes desyre hepe sutes stryues lawe vnto hym selfe gatherynge money spoylynge robbynge prelate also intendynge greatter subduynge yet howe great insolencie pryde hath folowed therof maner euery man knoweth aforesayd person lackynge cure obedyence dewe theyr prynce made stubburne dysobedyent without reuerence drede whome ought ryght worthelye subiectes obedyent taketh also hereof vnto selues occasyon lybertie syn large adde newe sprynge braunche sayd rote yt bysshop rome fulnes powre hath forbydden whiche haue ecclesiasticall benefyce euer without lycence make testamentes hath decreed goodes dyeth intestate couayed brought imedyatlye vnto see adde also greatter thynge deuyll large symonye althoughe fulfylled deade powre reserueth rente profytes frutes benefyces whatsoeuer place fyrste yere ar vacante gatheryng maner vnto hymselfe treasure worlde robbynge kyngdoms prouynces whiche prouynces ought dystrybuted mynystres gospell myserable person elles turned subsydie succour comune wealthe wherof taken yf nede shall requyre herefore haue ben ordayned assygned agayne itollerable thynge sayth legacyes bequest testamentes chrysten laye men passage beyonde see cause accordynge dysposycion certayne determynate persones whome call comyssaryes dothe appertayne ordrynge fulnes powre meruayle hereof seynge yt certayne bysshop amonge hath sayd hymselfe hath domynyon kynges prynces realmes comunyties notwithstandynge yt dede none aforesayd thynges doth appertayne vnto powre rote mo greuouser thynges shall chaunce sprynge vp whiche tolde dyuers nature one inconuenyent graunted namely suche one whiche incouenyenc may thought ymagyned aboute cyuyle actes co tayned harde thynge inconuenyences whatsoeuer chauce accordynge gentyle phylosopher arystotle full powre beynge due vnto hym foloweth may whatsoeuer helyste wherfore doth suspende dysanulle reuoke ye ordynacios lawes men owne pleasure thynge beynge extreme vttermoste incouenyent yt may worldly regyment gouernaunce well saynt phylosophers hath hated refused proued demostracyon xi chapytre fyrst dyccyon also largely confyrmed v dyccion auctoryte saynt augustyne ye vi chapytre fyrst epystle timothe fulnes powre permytted vnto hym yt whole body ye churche infectyd ordre ecclesiastycall iconomie broken cyuyle regyment gouernaunce letted vtterly troubled parte vpon whiche bysshop yf chrysten men wyll caste theyr iyes beseche whiche hath ben dusked bleared many adaye parte certayne couer cloke coloure sophistycall honesty shallse clerely selues soeuer hath visyted courte rome saye truely house marchaundyse horryble denne theues vse chrystes wordes whosoeuer hath visyted shal learne reporte great many credyble person yt made maner receptacle sanctuarye myscheuous men marchauntes bothe spyrytuall temporall thynge concourse symonyacall person countrees thynge bablynge noyse proctours pleader cause assaulte quarelers false accuser vexacion iuste men iustyce innocet person ioperdy least wyse greatly dyfferred put yf notable bye money laste beynge clene beggarde theyr money consumed themselues weryed innumerable labour compelled gyue ouer theyr ryghtful myserable cause lawes men thundre sounde lowde lawe supposycions aforesayde bysshop albeit hathe yet ben approued confyrmed wordes wrytynges haue euydentlye shewed neyther neadeth confyrmed yet withsta dynge tyme eleccion made publysshed electours hyther contynuallye hathe caused dothe cause hym selfe wryten named kynge romaynes dede accordynge trouth hathe ben also dothe admynystre thynges belongynge sayd kynge emperoure poyntes may also bounde ryght wherfore accordynge tale esope worthy marked well agreynge purpose serpent bysshoppe rome nowe albeit hathe ben exalted releued auaunced predecessours sayd ludouyke predecessours great pouertye vylenes oppressyon rebuke persecucyon vnto abundaunce temporall goodes hyghe dygnyte honoure powre tranquyllite yet lyke vnkynde persone one forgotten aforesayde benefytes hathe lyfted vp hym selfe agaynst aforesayd ludouyke fyrste lewde wonte maner spyttynge many wordes rebuke dysworshyp irreuerence agaynst sayd prynce yet offrynge venome poysone vnder apperaunce hony pretendeth olde crafte deceypte coloure apparaunce vertue charyte saythe certayne epystles whiche calleth decree wryteth speaketh suche thynges ende myght brynge agayne sayd ludouyke bypathe erroure vnto ryghte waye pathe truthe helthe regardynge hym selfe whiche speaketh neyther speaketh neyther whome speaketh bysshop beynge waye truth parteles equyte may say couenyently verely truly chryste texte vii mathewe viii luke seest thou strawe iye thy brother dost se bealme thyne owne iye sayst thou thy brother brother suffre caste strawe thyne iye haste bealme thyne owne iye thou hypocryte fyrste caste bealme thyne owne iye shalte thou se caste strawe thy brother iye good tree whiche bryngeth forth euylfruyte neyther euyll tree bryngyng forth good fruyte euery tree knowen owne fruyte dothe hypocryte euyltree brynge euery fruytes malyce seducyon dyscorde sencyble knowen men dothe go aboute defame vertuous man innocent catholyke praysed men wordes ignomine slaundre vnder false apperaunce coloure deuocyon charyte let hym fyrste caste owne mynde beynge ful darkenes blynde bealme wyt great ignoraunce erroure owne lewde affeccyon beynge maner oftynate durated let hym caste waye malyce furyous woodnes shall able se small faultes men maye exortacions monycyons metelye conuenyentlye caste men afterwarde aforesayd bysshop whiche vnder deceyptfull fayned wordes dothe intende amendment man cyuyle deathe destruccyon comune weale hathe powred forthe spredde abrode agaynst aforesayde moste chrysten prynce venomes poysons cyuyle lyfe whiche hathe supposed moste deadlye vnto hym hathe excomunycated hym pertyculerly cleue vnto hym hath also forbydden exercyse dyuyne seruyce vnto comunyties chrysten men whiche gyue aboute gyue helpe counsayle fauour vnto prynce beynge kynge romaynes lytle nothynge markyng regardynge counsayle saynt ambrose boke whiche intytled de sacerdotali dignitate ambrose treatynge texte paule thyrde chapytre fyrste epystle timothe yf man desyreth preesthode c amonge thynges viii chapytre sayde booke sayth thus brawler saye let preeste louse tonge raylynge euyll wordes lefte tonge whiche gyueth prayses god offereth vp deuyne seruyce brynge forth venome poyson braulynge stryfe semely bothe benedyccyon maledyccyon shulde yssue preestes mouthe agayne lefte tonge whiche god lawded man maye despraysed euyll spoken maye brynge forthe bothe swete water bytter water one fountayne sprynge conclusyon peraduenture shall sende forthe prycke stynge malyce whiche supposeth vtter extreme noyenge dystroyenge supposynge fasten vpon sayde prynce wytte certayne blasphemye called hym sentence thoughe verye fruytes haue co med proceded many hudred yeres ye seat rome holy father mayntayned holy father dede maye called madnes whiche hathe pronounced aforesayde prynce dothe cleue vnto hym dothe obeye hym fauoure hym kynge romaynes heretykes enemyes rebellyons vnto churche whiche sentence hathe depryued berefte ryght theyr temporalles bothe moueables vnmoueables makynge sayde temporalles comune aforesayde sentence vnworthelye called grauntynge also soeuer lyst entre vpon wynne get vyolence spreadynge abrode prouynces wordes elles wrytynges parchement hym selfe el certayne false preacher maye done lawfullye agayne condempnynge deathe grauntynge remyssyon forgyuenes al synnes paynes punysshementes crymes vnto kylle inuade bryngynge yf betaken prysoners lyue soeuer shall seruytute persones taketh moreouer graunteth greatest ecclesiasticall offyces bysshopryches archebysshop ryches patryarkeshypes meane smaller ecclesyastycall offyces also spendeth therto ecclesyastycall temporalles called benefyces treasure money churche maye rayse vp men enuye rebellyon warre dyscorde agayne sayd prynce dothe albeit dothe nothynge belonge auctoryte gyue forthe sentence forsayde thynges haue euydentlye declared besyde horryble malygnytes aforesayde exercyseth newe kynde wyckednes malyce whiche semeth manyfestlye smell heresye rayseth vp rebellyon agaynst sayde catholyke prynce owne subiectes leyge people assoylynge deuyllysshe sayenges wrytynges calleth al apostolycall wryttes othes fidelyte whiche ben verye truthe bounde ofte rehersed prynce suche maner absolucyons publyssheth preacheth euery certayne mynystres myschefes whiche suche maner exercyse hope truste promoted sayde bysshoppe vnto ecclesiasticall offyces benefyces p worke apostolyke diabolycall dede euydent accordynge sayde bysshoppe complyces ordynatours consenters executers worde wrytynge dede beynge blynde couytousnes pryde ambicyon fylled moste great iniquyte euydent men guydes leader gyue credence vnto folowe worke dede aforesayde sayenges wrytynges vnto fallynge goynge downe heedlynge dyche pytte deadly synnes fyrste manyfest open periurye afterwardes treason iniurye open playne men consequentlye causeth fall rauyne robbrye manslaughter maner kyndes myscheuous synnes whiche dyenge without repentaunce beynge begyled moste holy father mynysters yet excused god theyr grosse ignoraunce caste downe heedlonge drowned hell wytte pytte perpetuall dampned persones ought vndoubted euery man hathe reason able vse neyther bysshoppe rome neyther preeste may assoyle man suche maner lawfull othe outher gyuen made el promysed nowe euydent euery man wyll stande owne conscyence whiche troubled synystre croked affeccyon cause whiche bysshoppe rome pretendeth agaynst ye deuoute prynce lewes agaynst prynce lyke case resonable vnresonable vndyscrete vniust wherfore gydynge doctryne exhortacyon bysshoppe mynysters thynges eschewed auoyded vtterlye despysed thynge whiche leadeth bryngeth conclusyon vnto eternall deathe soules playnly openly contrary holsome doctryne wordes sentence apostle paule xiii romaynes vi ephesyanes vi fyrste epystle tymothe seconde thyrde chapytres seconde epystle tite apostle teacheth openly subiect true obedyence towarde kyng prynces whiche ye bysshop rome churche yet neuer taughte ought obeye theyr carnall lordes onely beynge good gentyle also beynge hasty frowarde saynte peter saythe fyrst canonycall epystle seconde chapytre howe moche ought obedyent whan bounde othe whiche thynge gloses also myndes sayntes place largely declare sayenge manyfestlye subiectes bounde oughte obey theyr lordes yea thoughe infydelles neuer frowarde euyll yet vnderstandynge meanynge suche thynges contrarye outher worde dede lawe god p vndoubted wordes workes whiche bysshop otherwyse called pope rome inueheth procedeth agayne emperour rome neyther comaundementes godes lawe neyther consonant agreable vnto rather dissonaunt manyfeste repugnaunt contrarye sayde lawe hathe ben shewed scrypture iiii v ix chapytours dyccyon agayne obeye bysshoppe rome bysshop reachynge preachynge thynges none thynge suffre rote regymentes gouernaunces cut vp bonde knot euery cyuylyte kyngdome losed broken sondre suppose suche maner roote bonde none thynge ought none otherwyse taken othe fydelyte prynces theyr subiectes eche dede fydelyte forsayde subiectes tullius saythe fyrste boke intytled de officiis fundament groundesell iustyce whiche fydelyte betwene gouernours subiectes whosoeuer gothe aboute dyssolue breake gothe aboute gette vnto hym selfe lesse thynge maye accordynge owne entent pleasure ouertourne destroye powre hyghe auctorytie prync gouernours cyuyle comunyte afterwarde brynge aforesayd subiectes owne seruytute bondage besydes also trouble peace tranquyllyte men lyueth cyuylye reason therof meanes depryue theyr suffycyet lyfe worlde fynallye brynge ben dysposed theyr mynde yf maye therto attende haue sayde vnto eternall dystruccyon theyr soules wherfore let chrysten men dyspyse beware vayne promyse pardon forgyuenes thynge clene cotrary agaynst ye lawe god pernycyous madde doctryne bysshop rome call vertue popysshe pardon truelye seduccyon soules bysshoppe rome complyces colledge clarkes cardynalles worse doctryne pharyseys regardynge chryste whiche counsayleth teacheth xv chapytre mathewe whan saythe chrysten men yet persone apostle suffre lette alone wytte pharyseys tyme supposed teacher moyses lawe erronyous opynyon vnderstandynge lawe maner contynuallye contrarye vnto chryste agaynst hym doctryne gospell pharyseys sygnyfyed vnderstanded pharysyes figure sophistical du sers thomatistes sophisticall false teacher holy scrypture whiche sorte persecutours romayne emperour innocet true chrysten people persone whome beynge membres chryste wycked persones wytte bysshoppe rome complyces also dothe persecute chryste dothe agaynst hym theyr dylygence laboure chryste sheweth cause afterwardes ought despyse false teacher sayth blynde guydes blynde men wherfore sayth yf one blynde man guyde blynde man bothe falleth dyche accordynge counsell teachynge chryste whiche teachynge euery chrysten man ought folowe false teacher lette alone despysed bothe blynde auaryce couetousnes pryde ambycion selues also guydes blynde men wytte couetouse proude rebellyous persones whiche false teacher also regardynge lystynge regarde precept ye apostle rather god sayenge playnlye without metaphore xiii chapytre romaynes let euery soule subiecte hygh power teache openlye soeuer resysteth ye power kynge hed prynce ye deuyll yea though aungell heuen yf possyble moche bysshop preeste popysshe pylled freer monke chanon peuysshe nunne subiectes rebelle agaynst theyr prynces gouernours suche persones rebellynge theyr gylefull vniuste perswasyons inducynge men rebellyon resyste ordynacyon god saythe apostle sayde chapytre soeuer saythe resysteth powre saye seculare gouernoure resysteth ordynacyon god whome apostle hathe prophesyed fourthe chapytre fyrste epystle timothe thyrde seconde epystle timothe whan sayde knowe thou laste dayes shall peryllous tymes towarde shall men louynge theyr owne selues couetous proude hyghe mynded blasphemous person obedyent theyr parentes vnder worde parentes comprehendynge prynces gouernours wherfore tully de officiis fyrste boke saythe prynces ben contrey parentes whose great benefytes bounden obedyent dysobedyent therfore theyr parentes moche saye dysobedyent prynces foloweth sayenge paule vnkynde persones full myscheyfe vnfaythfull kepynge promyse without copassyon goodnesse without peace traytoures lecherous persones cruell without benygnyte false accuser lewde toged frowarde swolne puffed vp pryde louers pleasure disobedient god hauynge dede face holynes saye apperynge thynges whiche honoure reuerence loue god effecte denyenge vertue wytte suche holynes deuocyon whiche thynge easy men knowe theyr workes accordynge texte vii chapytre mathewe take hede ware false prophetes whiche come vnto apparayle shepe inwardlye rauenynge wolues theyr fruytes shall knowe apostle saythe comformablye aforesayd counsayle precepte chryste persones auoyde thou saye beleue neyther obeye suche thynges ala pytuous case haue throughe apperaunce godlynes greatlye deceyued begyled men nowe trustynge vyolente powre whiche haue optayned gotten vnder apperaunce symylytude holynes partly mennes free gyfte great parte secrete preuy vsurpacyon nowe open vyolent vsurpacyon well auoyded eschewed doynge vyolence persecucyon chrystes faythful people whiche also beynge vnkynde proude without peace cruell dede suche maner persones poyntes apostle hathe descrybed affyrmynge good euyll lyght darkenes accordynge sayenge esaye prophete collacyon gyfte ecclesyastycall offyces bothe greatest meane sorte smallest exhybycion promysynge temporalles benefyces well mouables vnmouables tyethes whiche haue ben ordayned good ende abomynable conuencyon bargaynes hereof made styre vp agaynst chrysten prynces theyr owne subiectes also theyr owne cosens alyaunce straunge countrees beynge theyr subiectes whiche thynge althoughe theyr complyces nowe seme onelye agaynst emperoure emperours ar vexed bysshop rome kynges theyr bysshops clargye rome yet let prynces learne example sayde emperoure whiche hathe ben greatlye benefyciall bysshoppe rome churche thynges may lykelyhode chaunce vnto selues also aforesayde bysshoppe shall full busye thynges agaynst also whan occasyon suche assaulte shall offre selfe vnto hym without good affeccyon towardes euery man affyrmynge wordes wrytynges aforesayde prynces people subiectes gouernaunce coactyue iurysdyccyon fulnes powre calleth whiche vnaccordynglye ascrybeth vnto hym selfe day bysshops clargy wayte couetynge also desyrynge greatly brynge effecte wayteth suche tymes whiche appereth scysmes contencyons chrysten prynces people one rebellyon subiectes agaynst theyr soueraygnes ruler whiche sedycions contencions rebellyons hym selfe also procureth otherwhyles raysed styrred vp intente one partes beynge dyscorde betwene selues beynge weake feble beynge able resyste aduersarye parte may compelled beseche helpe ayde submyt hym selfe domynion albeit vnder fayned face apperaunce holynes deuocyon charyte semeth otherwhyles defende impotet weake person peraduenture wrongfully oppressed gyue vnto seculare fauour yet gyueth fauour excepte sure afore whiche nede fauour requyre wyll content come vnder gouernaunce seculare domynion hopynge therof conclusyon suche oppressynge enuye eche bothe part beyng varyaunce shall compelled come vnder domynion wherfore suche contencyons accyons auoyded whiche may brynge cause necessyte vnto man fauoure helpe laste turned destruccyon lybertye seruytude thraldom receyue sayde fauoure p maner sayd bysshop lytle lytle crepeth successyuely throughe kyngdoms worlde may last able subdue make subiecte vnto hym selfe empyres domynions worlde whiche thynge incessauntly desyreth dareth attempte suche maner process many togyther one tyme abydeth vntyll suche cunnynge poynte practicasyon tyme lytle lytle great seculer powre shall haue growen preuely vnto hym selfe dothe perceyue beleue may without iopardy ouercome powre empyres domynyons doth boldely open shewe forth vpon realmes sence meanynge tytle fulnes powre hath presumed take vpon hym doth expressely say forth prynces empyres subiecte domynyon coactyue iurysdyccion lykewyse sayth empyre ye romaynes nowe subiecte vnto hym wolde refuse although myght lawfully subiecte vnto hym doth pursue blasphemyes lyke sentence afore mayntayned agaynst emperour rome faythfull subiectes also vyolent armed powre euen vnto theyr vtter vndoynge thus meanes wayes sayd bysshop complyces haue welnere seduced studyeth brynge passe almayne brought prynces comunaltyes people italye contencions scysmes hathe begonne studyeth brynge passe contynuallye almayne hathe raysed vp certayne subiectes traytours vngracious persones seculer fauoures gyuynge ecclesynstycall offyces exhybycion tyethes money ben sone churche ye bysshoppe rome calleth vnto rebellyon agaynst emperoure rome procureth without ceasynge rayse vp soeuer maye great meane small person shall begyled hym whiche shall obeye hym calleth nameth sone churche true chrysten men soeuer co tynueth wyllynge cotynewe due faythfulnes obediet theyr prynce soueraygne nameth scysmatyk heretykes persecuteth ben heretyk ye bysshop rome calleth enemyes ye churche blasphemynge dyffamynge excomunycatynge moche euer may condepnynge theyr person goodes seculer sentence albeit suche maner iudgement suche fascyon belongynge hym suche one neyther lawe god neyther lawe man euydent thynges afore gone hathe ben rehersed heretofore p moste myscheuous thynge thynge whiche dothe greattest noyaunce hurte generally wherof haue spoken somwhat heretofore whiche maye passed ouer scylence hym wylleth falle lawe chryste gospell bysshoppe bysshop rome deuoureth shepe rome eternallye confoundeth deuoureth shepe chryste whome saythe comytted vnto hym selfe fedde holsome doctryne puttynge sayenge euyll good lyght darkenes graunteth mouthe wrytynge vnto men absolucyon maner synne absolucion synne payne wyll traytours theyr prynces payne vnto warreth certayne tyme outher horsebacke fote agaynst sayde chrysten subiectes emperoure rome obeyinge wyllynge obey hym constantlye beynge theyr kynge souerayne whome also beynge heretykes reblles crosse chryste pronouceth hym selfe men well worde mouthe wrytynge lawfull maner meanes impugne robbe fynally destroye whiche also abomynable herde preacheth openlye causeth preached openlye euery certayne deceyptfull false frears whiche hunger thryste ecclesyastycall dygnytes promocions yf acceptable god fyghte agaynst paganes partes ouer see destroye whiche deceyptfull false pardon forgyuenes sayde bysshoppe graunteth lykewyse vnto able feblenes bodye fulfyll performe myscheyfe yf theyr owne propre costes charge shall procure done men shall gyue suffycyent sume therfore vnto cursed vngracyous exactours gatherer notwithstandynge accordynge catholyke faythe relygyon let chrysten men shamed theyr madnes chryste man oughte doubte warre fyghte folysshe vayne absolucyon dothe profyte good dothe moche hurte vnto yet thus begyleth symple men accomplysshement owne wycked lewde desyres granntynge vnto thynge lyeth powre yea moreouer dothe meane brynge leade ryght waye vnto eternall deathe destruccyon theyr soules beynge inuadours landes prouynces countrees vniuste destroyer troubler peace quyetnes innocent chrysten men whome knowe trewe catholyke men defender theyr owne countree obseruers fydelyte theyr owne trewe lawfull lorde prynce gouernour sayd countre saye tobbynge kyllynge otherwyse impugnynge suche maner persones made champion deuyl chryste champion chryst champyons deuyll comytte fall vnto rauynes brynnynges theftes murthers fornycacyons aduoultryes well nere kyndes crymes trespass wherof euydente vndoubted deserue pardone forgyuenes rather calleth hi selfe vicar chryste ought truely called vycar deuyll made gyltye detters eternall dampnacyon doynge wherof thyng seduced sayenges probacyons holy scryptures whiche calleth hym selfe thoughe vycare chryste earthe blodsheder gylefull man beynge contented thynkynge ynoughe suche horryble thynges exercysed laye men comaundement throughe entysementes persuasyons hathe sent ouer certayne preeste one brother complyces whome call cardynall captayne cardynall abbot cheualrye great nombre company horseman fotemen prouynce lombardye also hathe sente lykewyse abbot certayne marchye italye called anchone impugne destroye faythful chrysten people whome wyll obey wycked vniuste co maundementes agaynst prynce dothe vexe without ceasynge maner aforesayde persecucyons hathe presumed wonte temeryte call sayenges wrytynges theyr deuoute prynce aforesayde ludouyke eperour called lorde abbot fauourer heretykes hathe compassyon cheryssheth accordynge powre fauourer heretykes whiche lyke v bysshoppe consumeth turneth ecclesiasticall temporalty whiche deuoute chrysten men aswell prynces theyr subiectes comunalties synguler persones haue appoynted ordayned sustentacyon mynystres gospell succurrynge releuynge impotent poore people also vniustlye chalengynge temporalles bequested testamentes vnto vertuouse v passage ouer see redemynge prysoners taken infydels lyke v saye chalengynge belongynge vnto powre gothe aboute tourne aforesayd v albeit worke mete successoure apostle preeste neyther dothe become preeste man consecrated vnto god moue weapon bydde warre made amonge chrystes faythfull people namelye vniustlye rather conuenyent exhortacions call agayne onely semely also forbeden lawe god preestes men warre people vnto concorde vnyte yf shall dyscorde debate amonge selues one hathe ben suffycyentlye shewed auctoryte apostle vexacyon conclusyon euerlastynge tornement dampnacyon also called pope euen nowe adayes mynystres calleth legate haue proceded late dayes contynuallye procede suche maner process laudable pleasaunt manashynge chryste verye trouth xviii chapytre mathewe sayth woo man slaunder cometh agayne chapytre soeuer shall offende one lytle one whiche beleueth expedyent hym mylnestone hanged necke drowned depthe see whiche sayenges nothynge markynge regardynge lykewyse regardeth monycions counsayles chryste beynge frowarde vnpenytente contynuallye without ceasynge dothe persecute blaspheme many noble mathewe shall gyue kayes kyngdome heuyns saythe whiche greued reherse certayne men vnderstandynge place example bysshoppe vnderstande thou take vnto selues somwhat note well word iherome vpon xvi mathewe pryde hyghe mynde pharyseys suppose selues condempne innocentes lose assoyle malefactours gylty persones foloweth afterwardes purpose albeit dede afore god sentence preestes lyfe persones accused soughte god therfore dothe folowe iudgement suche maner preeste bysshoppe churche beynge vniuste contrarye equytye wherfore blasphemyes hym complices dredde feared chrysten man haue sayde tyme come shall expresse tytle agaynst resydue prynces whan shall perceyue se sedycyon theyr realmes shal se also hymselfe hathe vyolent powre vsurpe occupye wynne fulnes powre throughe cowardenes whiche bysshop rome successours aforesayde seate preestes deacon spyrytual mynystres whome speake wordes enemyes cal god wytnesse agaynst body protestacion marsilius padway soule rather vnto father moreouer also honest maners dyscyplynes beynge corrupted maner kyndes vyces wantonnes myschefes errours haue vtterlye possessyd occupyed myndes bodyes bothe men woman successyon theyr chyldren cut seynge haue made cheyfe pryncypall apostle vnderstanded onelye apostle whiche tyme shulde strengthed peter chrysten men lytle foloweth glose repentaunce obtayned wyt peter pryncypall bysshop ye worlde conomye admynystracion chryste dyd gyue vnto essencyall dygnyte sayd go therfore teache nacyons gyuen essencyall dygnyte vnto afore tyme case put one lyke tyme gyuen dygnytes auctorytes yet saye bysshoppes preestes wherfore apostle saythe imedyatlye folowynge therfore yf shall haue seculer iudgementes ordeyne sette iudges whiche contemptyble churche saye rebuke none wyse man amonge whiche therfore saythe yf shall haue seculer iudgementes suche iudgementes rather despysed yf haue suche iudgementes ordayne sette gyue iudgement contemptyble saye vndyscrete vyle persones whiche churche saye thus haue done reason wherof brother myghte compelled haue recourse agayn vnto infydels hethen iudges apostle repreueth rebuketh speakynge ironycallye saye meanynge contrarye wordes dothe sounde semely conuenyent shulde therofre sayth speake shamefastnes reuerence saye comaunde speake shulde asshamed oughte ashamed one man amonge wyse able iudge betwene brother brother must nedelye make fooles iudges yet fooles made iudges rather shulde go heathen iudges yf wante wyse men amonge saye wyse man amonge dothe one brother stryue brother iudgement whiche euyll thynge yea afore heathen iudges worse thynge elles thus therfore yf shall haue seculer iudgementes c apostle sayd myght iudge leaste smalest thynges therfore doth nowe determyne ordayned appoynted iudges determynynge suche tytle full power whiche pryncypallye grauted hym sayth chryst person saynt peter haue sayde laste chapytre fyrst dyccyon hath ben reasonable cause repeted oftentymes rehersed verye many chapytres seuerallye haue euydently shewed proued fyrste dyccyon certayne humayne worldly reason haue also confyrmed iiii v chapytres seconde dyccyon testymonyes euerlastynge trouth also exposycyons declared shewed semeth appereth rote synguler malygnyty ofte named prohemy preface suffycyently cut vp wherfore nowe ye braunches twygges graffes dyscorde stryfe whiche pestylence myschefe hath realmes yt hensforth shal stopped hauyng entraunce comunytes p clere euydent inferrynge certayne conclusyons necessarely folowyng thynges whiche haue ben determyned ii fyrst dyccyons partes boke attencyon dylygent markyng conclusyons prynces gouernoures also theyr subiectes may sooner easely attayne ende purposed entended boke seconde chapytre p whiche sayde conclusyons inferred wyll make socyetes felowshyppes men amonge selues maye beste holden kepte consydered ioyned togyther certayne contynuall fauoure loue offycers ruler multytude comunes eache establesshed made fyrme sure without
